/* Mem: 5396 MB. Coordinator: dev04.vpc.cloudera.com. */
select
  c_name,
  c_custkey,
  o_orderkey,
  o_orderdate,
  o_totalprice,
  sum(l_quantity)
from
  customer,
  orders,
  lineitem
where
  o_orderkey in (
    select
      l_orderkey
    from
      lineitem
    group by
      l_orderkey
    having
      sum(l_quantity) > 300
    )
  and c_custkey = o_custkey
  and o_orderkey = l_orderkey
group by
  c_name,
  c_custkey,
  o_orderkey,
  o_orderdate,
  o_totalprice
order by
  o_totalprice desc,
  o_orderdate
limit 100
